name:Yâ€uâ€eâ€râ€sâ€hâ€uâ€iâ€zâ€hâ€oâ€nâ€gâ€yâ€oâ€u

info:Stayed in September 2023

info:45 Reviews
rating:4
posted:Posted September 11, 2023
msg:The hotel is located on a mountain, quiet and has good design taste. It can be used as an experience for people who have lived in the city for a long time. If you travel frequently, it is not necessary. Bali and other places are full of such hotels, and the price/performance ratio is several times higher. The flaw in the design of the hotel is that the ventilation of the stone house is not considered enough. The decorative stone wall in front of the courtyard blocks the air flow. There are only floor-to-ceiling glass windows in the house, which seems to let in enough light, but in fact there is no circulating wind. Moreover, in summer There are so many mosquitoes that we have to close the door tightly. It is a pity that we can only rely on air conditioning in the countryside. The price is five-star, and the service is only at the level of a B&B. It may be due to lack of training or too many tourists. The young staff in each position showed a hint of impatience, including the singer who sang wrong words in the evening. For a hotel at this price, the transportation is so inconvenient that there is no car to at least send it down the mountain. There are many guests with children. The only restaurant is not only expensive but also has few food suitable for children. As for the problems in the room, the basin is cracked, the wall is moldy, the toilet remote control does not work, and the garden lights are out of control, just to name a few. Four points are given for encouragement.

First of all, the housekeeper did not pick me up in the parking lot. The car had to be driven to the hotel entrance and then back to the parking lot to park. Then I entered the room. The room design was relatively cramped. I specially booked a room with a balcony. As a result, the distance between the buildings was very close. Apart from the view from the balcony, There is no view from the roof of the house in front. He said that dinner must be reserved in advance at the restaurant. When I arrived at 5 o'clock, there was no one in the restaurant. I finally found someone later and said that it would only start at 6:30. Later I learned that it normally starts at 5:30 because there was a team building and the chefs were all Went there to serve. In the evening, it was said that there would be a concert starting at 8 o'clock. We went there on time and only the resident singer was there. We wanted to order something to eat. It took 20 minutes for the service staff to arrive. Later, the team members were full of wine and food and played the music. It will become their KTV, so take the kids away quickly. I would like to ask, there is nothing wrong with undertaking team building, are individual tourists not human beings? name:Gâ€uâ€eâ€sâ€tâ€ â€Uâ€sâ€eâ€r
info:Stayed in October 2021
info:Family
info:12 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted October 27, 2021
msg:Hidden on the mountainside, this place was originally a Buyi village in Huangguoshu ****ouzhai. Although it has a history of hundreds of years, it was gradually abandoned as the villagers moved down the mountain. Later, there was the Village Xiao Resort.

Thank you customer service Sisi for the service before and after check-in~

Letâ€™s talk about the guest rooms. Because they are remodeled from different old buildings, the size, layout and functions of the guest rooms are different. It is important to choose a room according to your needs.
I learned in advance that there is no extra bed service. In order to live comfortably, I chose a single-family suite. The tatami tea seat in the small living room can be transformed into a big bed for the brothers at night.
The bathtub is set in the sun room outside the corridor, which not only meets the needs of sunbathing, but also avoids the cool breeze in the mountains. It can be described as everything.

The location of our building is also very good. It is located in the center front row of the guest room tribe, adjacent to the restaurant activity area and the swimming pool area. The supporting terrace is located on the high rise outside the door, with a unique and wide view.

The point is that there are layers of hanging plants under our terrace. Passing guests love to stop and take pictures. In fact, there is also a public laundry room in the resort. Guests can do laundry, dry clothes, iron clothes, and bring children. Great convenience for families traveling.

The restaurant in Cunxiao is open to the public. As far as the taste is concerned, it is worthy of a special trip for nearby tourists. The outdoor air is fresh, the indoors are clean and comfortable, and there are more dishes than Yueshan B&B. We are satisfied with every meal. We are not blind. Step on thunder.

By the way, we went on the National Day holiday, and there was a bonfire party after nightfall. The local Bouyei elder sisters would come and dance with the guests. You can't help but want to dance twice.

Real evaluations, both positive and negative, with shortcomings for friends to learn from later. Advantages: The environment is first-class, the resort is very large, unique and unique, and the scenery is beautiful. The weather is pleasant here in early October, cool and not stuffy. The bed and pillows were very comfortable. The service staff were very nice and enthusiastic. They also gave me a small gift when I checked out. It should be the local specialty peanut candy, which is delicious. The food in the restaurant tastes good too. Each room has its own small courtyard, which is very quiet and private, and will not be disturbed. In the evening, a bonfire party is held to dance with the Miao aunties. There are free tea, fruits, and snacks in the room. There is an outdoor swimming pool, the children had a lot of fun, parking is very convenient, and the navigation is easy to find. The security guard in the parking lot was also very nice. This is a great place especially suitable for couples, families and children to travel. It only takes about ten minutes to drive from Huangguoshu Waterfall Scenic Area. Letâ€™s talk about the shortcomings: (Maybe itâ€™s just me who had some problems with this room, but it doesnâ€™t mean everything)
1. The bath water in Room 2303 where I stayed would flow outside, making it so slippery that I almost fell;
2. There is a loud noise when the toilet is filled with water;
3. The scale is out of power and the details of the room inspection are not in place;
4. The window facing the bedside, first of all, the curtains are not made of completely blackout material, and! The point is that if you can't pull it all the way, you'll be woken up by the light in the morning, which is very unfriendly to people who sleep in late. (Figure 5)
5. There are many mosquitoes, and many flying insects that have never been seen fly into the room. This is understandable. After all, in a mountain village, although the room has electric mosquito coils, it is still recommended that the young people come prepare some peppermint oil, etc.
The overall evaluation is 4.5. I hope the management can improve these small problems and make them better and better.
